 sieji ne gail par yah bhi aarope lagaaya ki vah urvarak companiyon ko riyayati gas kaa gaiyr-urvarak banane main upyog se rokane main asafal rahi
 In its report tabled in Parliament, the CAG accused Gail of being fined 29 for acquiring more gas for one month from Reliance Industries
 78 karod vasuulne main asafal rahi
 The report said that aside from the directive of the ministry, GAIL supplied natural gas at a subsidized rate to ineligible customers who supply electricity at commercial rates to their customers
 sieji ne kaarobaari saal 2010-11 kii report main kaha, "gail ne sarkaar prashasit keemat tantra (apiem) ke tahat gas kii aapurti aisi bijli utpaadak companiyon ko kii, jinhone 2006 main apane graahakon ko vanijyik daron par aapurti kii
 This leads to 246 in the gas pool account
 16 karod rupee kii kam vasuuli hui, isse aise utpaadakon ko itani hi raashi kaa anuchit laabh mila or yogya graahakon ko yah laabh nahin mil paaya
 " sarkaar prashasit gas sirf un bijli companiyon ke liye he, jo grid ko aapurti karne ke liye bijli kaa utpaadan karte hai or jinka vitaran saarvajanik upabhokta companiyon kii marfat hota he
 The CAG said that GAIL also failed to develop such a system to determine how much gas was used by any fertilizer companies in the manufacture of non-fertilizer products and the payment for that should be at the market rate and not the discounted rate
 On
 tippaniyan The price of gas used for non-fertilizer was to be charged at the market rate from January 1, 2009
 sieji ne kaha ki gaiyr urvarak utpaadon ke liye gas ke upyog ke mudde ke samaadhaan main tel mantralay or rasayan tathaa urvarak mantralay main talmail kaa abhaav tha
 The report stated, "this situation led to a short recovery in the gas pool account for the period July 2005 to December 2008 and more concessions on fertilizers were paid by the government
" " The CAG also accused Gail of failing to prevent fertilizer companies from using subsidized gas to make it non-fertilizer
 sansad main pesh apni report main sieji ne gail par aarope lagaaya ki vah reliance industries se ek maheene tak adhik gas hasil karne ke liye jurmaana ke taur par 29
 78 crore failed to be recovered
 report main kaha gaya ki mantralay ke nirdesh se alag jaakar gail ne un ayogy graahakon ko riyayati dar par prakritik gas kii aapurti kii, jo apane graahakon ko vanijyik dar par bijli kii aapurti karte hai
 The CAG reported in the FY 2010-11 report, "GAIL supplied gas under the Government Administered Price Mechanism (APM) to power generating companies that supplied commercial rates to their customers in 2006
 isse gas pool khate main 246
 There was a short realization of Rs 16 crore, due to which such producers got an unfair advantage of the same amount and eligible customers could not get this benefit
 " Government-administered gas is only for those power companies that produce electricity to supply to the grid and which are distributed through public consumer companies
 sieji ne kaha ki gail aisi pranali kaa vikaas karne main bhi asafal rahaa, jisase yah tay kiya ja sake ki kisi urvarak companiyon ne gaiyr urvarak utpaada ke nirmaan main kitni gas kaa upyog kiya or uske liye bhugtan bazaar dar par ho, na ki riyayati dar par
 The comments gaiyr urvarak ke liye upyog kiye gaye gas kii keemat ek janvari 2009 se bazaar dar par lee jaani thi
 The CAG said that there was a lack of coordination between the Oil Ministry and the Ministry of Chemicals and Fertilizers to address the issue of the use of gas for non-fertilizer products
 report main kaha gaya, "is sthiti ke kaaran july 2005 se disambar 2008 kii avadhi gas pool khate main kam vasuuli hui or sarkaar dwaara urvarkon par adhik riyaayat kaa bhugtan kiya gaya

 Shalini Yadav has inherited politics
 shalini ke sasur shyaam laal yadav congress ke diggaj netaa rahe hai, jinka congress hi nahin balki gandhi parivaar se kabhi sidhaa sarokaar hua karata tha
 Due to this, Congress gave Shalini Yadav the mayor's ticket in 2017 from Varanasi seat
 shalini bijepi kii mridula jaiswal se bhale hi haar gai, lekin ek lakh chaudaa hajaar vot hasil karne main kaamyaab rahi thi

 saal, 1957 or 1962 main congress ke raghunatha singh is seat se jite the, lekin 1967 main CPM ke satyanarayan singh ne yahaan kabza kar liya

 1980 main congress kii vaapasi hui, or kamalapati treepathi ne is seat par kabza kiya, or phir 1984 main bhi congress ke hi shyaamalaal yadav ne varanasi se jeet hasil kii

 vahiin isaki bahan mobile main biji thi

 teen faislon kaa udhaaharan dete hue faisle main likhaa gaya he ki yah sadak yaa pul banane ke tender kaa maamla nahin he, raksha se sambandhit kharid kii prakriya kaa maamla he
 Therefore, the scope of judicial review becomes limited
 faisla angrezi main he isliye anuwaad karne main chook ho sakati he, phir bhi yahi laga ki adaalat raksha maamle ke tender ko sadak or pul ke tender kii prakriya main fark kar rahi he
